posted:Posted October 3, 2023
msg:We were visiting Shenzhen and Hong Kong during Chinese National Holiday. As long as our plan was to visit Hong Kong the hotels location near to LuoHu border pass make it very good option for us. 
We had concern about noisy environment because a railway station is just over the street. But the hotel is calm. 
Staff is friendly, helpful and patient :). 
Unfortunately, there is one big drawback.
While we were booking the hotel It was told that hotel has electric charging station for electric cars. Well, it has....for TESLAs only. At the underground parking I found a number of "universal" chargers, but they were not operational. There were traces of flood everywhere at the parking area. It seems hotel suffered a lot during last big typhoon about one month ago. 
Moreover, at the service desk I didn't received any information as to where I could charge my car. I spent rest of the evening looking for the charge station, which I found 200 meters out of the hotel between the train station and border pass main building at the second level. 
Well, I guess hotel staff should know about this.
Except this, our stay in the hotel was very pleasant and relaxing....they have even a gym and a swimming pool! :)
My recommendation to consider a stay in the hotel to all who's gong to spend several days in Shenzhen and Hong Kong.
